Ordinary hard drives are made of metal and use mechanism to process things. Ordinary hard drives can be slow and may lead to system crashes if not treated properly. I've been researching about this all over, and this thing could be down the chute very soon. Don't trust buying hard drives that use metal and mechanism to process things. It boots slowly, opens programs slowly, and may lead to system crashes after several months or years owned. The best thing to do is to purchase a Solid State Drive rather than buying an ordinary hard drive.
